1b1(mdo sde): / drug snang du/ A ma hA
1b2(mdo sde): nA ma swA 'a skar du/ 'a gas
1b1(mdo sde): yosu mya ngan las 'das pa chen po zhes bya ba'i mdo// bam/ 
2a1(mdo sde): thog ma/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
2a2(mdo sde): la phyag 'tshala'o// 'di skad bdag gis thos padus gcig na
2a3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das/ rtsa mchog gi grong khyer skyesabu stobs po
2a4(mdo sde): 'byung ba'i gnas/ klung ha ri la ba te'i 'gram/ shing sa la dang gnyis kyi bar
2b1(mdo sde): na dge slong chen po'i dge 'dun brgya stong phrag brgyad du snyed kyis yongs su bskor nas/ mdun du bdar te thabs
2b2(mdo sde): gcig tu bzhugs so// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das dpyid zla 'bring po'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin par/ yongs su
2b3(mdo sde): mya ngan las 'da' bar gshe gas su nyed na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyi rlabs kyi
2b4(mdo sde): gsung chen pos srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du kun tu khyab par sems can thams cad la so so'i skad du/ gsung
2b5(mdo sde): 'di skad ces grags par gyur to// deng de bzhin gshegs pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skye bo rnas 'jug
3a1(mdo sde): sems can gyi skyabs dang / mgon tu gyur pa/ sems can thams cad
3a2(mdo sde): la sras sgra gcan 'dzin dang 'dra bar mnyam par gzigs pa/ sems can gyi skyabs dang / dpung gnyen
3a3(mdo sde): dang rten dang gnas su gyur pa dang yongs su ma ngan las 'da'o// so so'i skye bo
3a4(mdo sde): dag the tsom dang som nyir gyur pa yod na/ do zhu zhing dri ba'i dus nang gi tha ma 'di ro zhu zhing
3a5(mdo sde): gsol cig/ ces pa'i gsung gi yongs su grags par gyur to// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das snga de'i
3a6(mdo sde): dus kyi tshe/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od rnam pa sna tshogs bkye ba ni/ 'di lta ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / 
3b1(mdo sde): dmar po dang / dkar po dang / shel lta bus/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di dang / phyogs bcu'i
3b2(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bar du yongs su snang bar byas nas/ de dag na gnas pa'i lam rgyud drug gi sems can dag/ 'od zer des
3b3(mdo sde): reg ma thag tu kha na ma tho ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad byang bar gyur to// de'i tshe so so'i skye bo dag de lta bu'i ltas mthong zhing
3b4(mdo sde): thos nas/ mya ngan chen pos yid// gdungs te/ dus gcig tu chong 'debs shi ngus nas/ 'di skad du/ e ma'o
3b5(mdo sde): shin tu byams pa'i pha mar gyur pa/ kyi hud kyi hud mya ngan las 'das sam/ zhes smras nas/ thal mos mgo dang brang la rdebs te cho
3b6(mdo sde): de rdung ngo // kha cig ni lus kyang rab tu 'dar zhing ba spu kun langs nas/ skad kyis brnangs pa tsam du dus so// de'i tshe na sa chen po dang / 
3b7(mdo sde): ri dang / rgya mtsho yang rab tu g.yos shing 'khrugs so// de nas sems can de dgacig la cig spro bsring zhing mya ngan bsang ba'i phyir/ 'di skad
4a1(mdo sde): dukye grogs po dag mya ngan ma byed par myur du rtsa mchog gi grong khyer skyes bu stobs po che 'byung ba'i gnas/ de bzhin gshegs
4a2(mdo sde): pa ga la ba der 'dong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ de bzhin gshegs pa yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' bar/ 
4a3(mdo sde): 'jig rten na bskal pa gcig gam/ bskal pa gcig 'grib kyi bar du bzhugs par gsol du 'deng ngo zhes smras so// lo la ni gcig gi lag pa la
4a4(mdo sde): gcig gis 'jus nas/ 'di skad du/ 'jig rten stong ste/ sems can gyi bsod nams zad pas/ mi dge ba'i las 'jig rten
4a5(mdo sde): du 'byung bar gyur gyis/ grogs po dag de bzhin gshegs pa ni ring por mi thogs par yongasu mya ngan las 'da' bar gshegs
4a6(mdo sde): nges kyis/ bdag cag myur du 'deng ngo zhes smra'o// la la ni 'di skad du/ 'jig rten stongs so// 'jig rten stong so// bdag cag la deng slan
4a7(mdo sde): cad ni mgon dang skyabs med de/ dbul 'phongs par gyur to// dang kho nar bla na mang bu'i bcom ldan 'das dang yongasu bral bas/ da slan cad
4a8(mdo sde): the tsom dang / som nyi za ba su la zhu zhes smra'o// de'i tshe na chad med pa'i nye gnas chen po/ tshe dang ldan pa ka t+ya ya na chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa bku
4b1(mdo sde): la dang / tshe dang ldan pa bsnyen dga' bo la sogs pa dge slong chen po de dag kyang / sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg pas lus kun 'dar zhing mi bzod pa tsam du rab tu g.yos te
4b2(mdo sde): sems kyang myos nas/ cho nge 'debs shing / de lta bu'i sdug bsngal rnam pa sna tshogs kyis non par gyur to// de'i tshe gzhan yang dge slong brgya stong phrag brgyad cu snyed thams cad
4b3(mdo sde): kyang dgra bcom pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pa/ bya ba byas pa/ nyon mongs pa yongs su spangs pa/ dbang po thams cad rab tu dul ba/ klu'i rgyal po chen po ltar mthu che ba/ 
4b4(mdo sde): stong pa'i shes rab dang ldan pa/ phyis bdag gi don rab da tu rnyed pa/ tsan dan gyi tshal ltar/ tsan dan gyis yongs su bskor ba/ seng ge'i rgyal po ltar/ sang ges
4b5(mdo sde): yongs su bskor ba/ de lta bu'i tshad med pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi sras yang dag pa sha stag go/ de dag kyang snga dro nyi ma shar ma thag
4b6(mdo sde): tu gnas nas byung ste/ so shing 'cha ba na sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg nas/ gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ grogs po dag myur du kha lag khrus shig ces smras so// de skad
4b7(mdo sde): ces smras ma thag tu lus kyi ba spu kun langs nas/ lus la khyab par khrag gis rgyas pa ni/ me tog pa la sha lta bur gyur te/ mig mchis mas gang nas/ sdug bsngal
4b8(mdo sde): chen po myong bar gyur to// de dag thams cad kyang sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i don gyi phyir/ theg pa chen po don dam pa stong pa nyid la rnal 'byor du bsgrub
5a1(mdo sde): pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pas thabs su dgongs te gsungs pa dag bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam pa sna tshogs su chos ston pa rgyun mi gcad pa'i/ 
5a2(mdo sde): phyir sems can thams cad yongs su gdul ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der myur du dong nas/ spyi bos sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong
5a3(mdo sde): du bskor nas thal mo sbyar te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang ku ta li'i bu mo dge slong ma dpal bzangs dang / dge slong ma bsten dga' ma dang / dge slong
5a4(mdo sde): ma rgya mtsho'i blo gros la sogs te/ dge slong ma khri phradag drug cu snyed thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ zagapa zad pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pa/ bya ba byas
5a5(mdo sde): pa/ nyon mongs pa yongs su spangs pa/ dbang po rab tu dul ba/ klu chen po ltar gzi brjid rab tu che ba/ stong pa nyid kyi shes rab dang ldan po sho stag/ 
5a6(mdo sde): ste/ de dag kyang snga dro'i dus kyi che/ nyi ma thog ma shar ba na/ lus kyi ba spu kune skyi bung zhes byed nas/ lus la khyab par khrag gis rgyas pa ni/ me tog pa la shwa lta
5a7(mdo sde): bur gyur te/ mig mchi mas yongasu gang nas/ sdug bsngal chen po myong bar gyur to// de dag kyang sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ theg pa chen
5a8(mdo sde): de'i don dam pa'i stong pa nyid la rnal 'byor du bsgrub pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pas thabs su dgongs te gsungs pa dag bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam pa sna tshog su chos
5b1(mdo sde): ston pa rgyun mi bcad pa'i phyir/ sems can thams cad yongs su gdul ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der myur du dong nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi bos
5b2(mdo sde): phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor nas thal mo sbyar te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// dge slong ma de dag gi nang na/ dge slong ma kha gcig ni byang chub sems
5b3(mdo sde): dpa' ste/ mi'i nang na klu lta bu sa bcu rab tu non pa/ mi g.yo ba la gnas pa/ sems can gdul ba'i phyir bud med kyi lus ston kyang rtag tu tshad med pa bzhi la nan tan byed/ 
5b4(mdo sde): pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pas/ sangs rgyas kyi skur yang sprul pa sha stag go// de'i tshe gzhan yangaklung gang gcig gi bye ma snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa'
5b5(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po mi'i nang na klu lta bu/ sa bcu rab tu non pa mi g.yo ba la rab tu gnas pa/ thabs rgya lus ston pa sha stag la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems
5b6(mdo sde): dpa' rgya mtsho dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' blo gros mi zad pa la sogs te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gis thog mar drangs nas/ thams cad
5b7(mdo sde): kyang theg pa chen po la bkur sti byed pa/ theg pa chen po la rab tu gnas pa/ theg pa chen po la shin tu mkhas pa/ theg pa chen po la shin tu mos pa/ theg pa chen po
5b8(mdo sde): la shin tu srung ba/ 'jig rten du bcas pa thams cad kyi sems dang sbyor ba/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su ma grol ba grol bar yi dam 'cha' ba/ 'das pa'i dus na bskal pa grangs
6a1(mdo sde): da rgyal mas su gru pa/ snang pa sa su na/ mthal bgrul ba skyed / ga mchag sa ma rgyu / 
6a2(mdo sde): tsham/ mdzangs pa'i dus su chos kyi 'khor la nor bar 'gyur ba/ rgyan chen pos shin tu brgyan pa/ de lta bu'i yon tan chad med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams ca
6a3(mdo sde): mthu gcig pa dang 'dra bar lbu ba sha stag go// de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma shar ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg ma thag tu/ lus kyi baspu kun langs te/ lus la khyab par
6a4(mdo sde): khrag gis rgyas pa ni dza ltar me tog pa la sha lta bur gru / mig mchims yong su gang nas/ sdug bsngal myong bar gyur to// de dag kyang sems can thams cad la pan
6a5(mdo sde): pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ theg pa chen po don das pastong pa nyid la rnal 'byor du bsgrub pa'i phyir/ bzhin gshegs pas thabs su dgongs te gsungs pa
6a6(mdo sde): bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam pa sna tshogs su chos bston pa rgyun mi gcang pa'i phyir/ sems can thams cad yongs su gdul ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der myur du
6a7(mdo sde): nas phyin pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor te/ thal mo sbyar nas/ sti stong dang / bcas pas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// 
6a8(mdo sde): de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA gnyis kyi bye ma snyed kyi dge bsnyen pa khrims lnga yongs su bsrung ba la 'di lta ste/ dge bsnyen gzi brjid dri ma med par grags pa'i rgyal po dang / dge bsnyen
6b1(mdo sde): legs pa'i yon tan la sogs pas thog mar drangs te/ thams cad kyang gnyen por gyur pa'i chos la shin tu mos pa ni 'di lta ste/ sdug bsngal ba dang / bde ba dang / rtag pa dang / 
6b2(mdo sde): mi rtag pa dang / yongs su dag pa dang / ma dag pa dang / bdag dang / bdag med pa dang / nges pa dang / ma nges pa dang / skyibasu 'gro ba dang / skyab su mi 'gro ba dang / yon dang / 
6b3(mdo sde): sems can ma yin pa dang / ther zug dang / ther zug ma yin pa dang / bde ba dang / bde ba ma yin pa dang / 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas pa dang / chad pa dang // 
6b4(mdo sde): chad pa ma yin pa dang / mya ngan las 'da' ba dang / mya ngan las 'da' ba ma yin pa dang / lhag ma dang / lhag ma ma yin pa la sogs te gnyen por 'gyur ba
6b5(mdo sde): chos 'di dag la rtog par shin tu mos pa sha stag go/ gzhan yang bla na med pa'i theg pa chen po la thos par mos pa ji ltar thos pa bzhin du gzhan la yang stan nus
6b6(mdo sde): pa/ tshul khrims yongs su bsrung ba/ theg pa chen po la skom pas gsungs pa ltar mos pa/ bdag kyang shin tu ngoms la/ skom pas gdungs pa gzhan yang ngoms par byed pa
6b7(mdo sde): bla na med pa'i ye shes la shin tu 'jug pa/ theg pa chen po la mos pa/ theg pa chen po la shin tu srung ba/ 'jig rten pa thams cad kyi sems dang / shin tu sbyor ba/ ma rgal ba
6b8(mdo sde): sgrol ba/ ma grol ba 'grel pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad par 'tsho ba/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su chos kyi 'khor lo shin tu skor ba/ rgyan chen pos rnam par
7a1(mdo sde): brgyan pa/ sems shin tu zab mo'i rol mos pa/ tshul khrims yongs su dag pa thams cad de lta bu'i yon tan dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la/ 
7a2(mdo sde): snying rje chen po'i sems skyed cing / bu gcig pa dang 'dra bar gnyi su med par snyoms pa sha stag go// de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma shar ma thag tu/ 'od zer gyis reg nas/ de bzhin
7a3(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i dpur zhugs la bzhen pa'i phyir/ thams cad kyis so so nas spros kyi shing khri phrag du ma bshams pa la 'di lta ste/ spos kyi shing tsan dan dang / a ka ru dang / 
7a4(mdo sde): 'go shir sha tsan dan dang / lha'i shing bskyong can la sogs pa'o// shing de dag kyang mdzes pa'i ri mo dang ldan zhing / rin po che sna bdun gyis rnam par brgyan pa/ 
7a5(mdo sde): 'od shin tu 'tsher zhing gsal ba ni dper na/ ri mo mkha na gyis mtshon sna tshogs bkye ba dang 'dra ste/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis/ kha dog sngon po dang / ser/ 
7a6(mdo sde): po dang / dmar po dang / dkar por ldan te/ 'gro ba mang po mthong na dga' bar 'gyur ba sha stag go/ shing rnam pa mang po de dag la gzhan yang rnam pa sna tshogs kyi spos kyi 'del
7a7(mdo sde): gu dang / gur khum dang / a ka ru dang / pog la sogs pas yongs su bskus la/ me tog rnam pa sna tshogs kyis gtor cing brgyan pa ni/ 'di lta ste/ me tog chud pa sa dang / me tog ku 6
7a8(mdo sde): nyi rdzag gas re ka la sogs pa'o// shing de dag la gzhan yang tshon rnam pa lnga dang ldan pa'i bdan shin tu 'jam zhing mdzes pas yongs su sbyangs pa ni/ dper na lha'i na bza' ke'u
7b1(mdo sde): sha sa 'am shu ma lta bu'o// spos kyi shing de dag kyang rin po che'i shing rtas bsdus te/ rin po che'i shing rtang dag las kyang / 'od rnam pa sna tshogs 'byung ba ni 'di lta ste/ sngon
7b2(mdo sde): dang ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po'o// shing rta'i gnya' shing dang / bar rdang la sogs pa'ang / rin po che sna bdun gyis rnam par spras te/ shing rta de re re yang
7b3(mdo sde): rta bzhi bzhis drangs so// rta de dag kyang mgyogs khyad rlung dang 'dra'o// shing rta de re re'i mdun na/ rin po che sna bdun gyi rgyal mtshan lnga bcu snyed mang te/ gser gyi dra bas bla
7b4(mdo sde): rer bres so// shing rta de re re steng yang rin po che gdugs lnga bcu snang bres so// shing rta re re re la yang me tog gi phreng ba sbyangs pa ni 'di lta ste/ me tog ung
7b5(mdo sde): bal dang / me tog ku mu dang / me tog pad+mo dang / pund ri ka rnams te/ 'dab ma ni gser ge sar ni rdo rje la byas to// me tog gi ge sar de dag gi nang
7b6(mdo sde): na yang bung ba nag po ldong zhing rtse'o// gzhan yang sgra skad shin tu snyan pa dang / de ma yin pa mi rtag pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / stong pa nyid dang / bdag med pa'i sgra yang 'byin to// 
7b7(mdo sde): de dag las gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'i sngon spyad pa spyod pa'i sgra dang / gzhan yang rol mo rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sgra grag pa ni 'di lta ste/ glu dang gar dang / gling bu dang / dgu po rgyud mangs
7b8(mdo sde): dang / seru dang / shaur dang / rnga'i sgra rnams so// rol mo'i sgra de las gzhan yang 'di skad du/ kyi hud kyi hud 'jig rten stong so zhes zer ba'i sgra yang byung ngo // shing rta re re re'i mdun na
8a1(mdo sde): dge bsnyen rin po che sna bzhi'i khri'u thogs pa re re yod de/ khri'u de'i steng na rnam pa sna tshogs kyi me tog spungs pa ni 'di lta ste/ me tog ud pa la dang / 
8a2(mdo sde): ku mu ta dang / pad+mo dang / pun da ri ka dang / gur khum dang / byug spos dang / bdug spos la sogs pa mchog tu gyur/ phul du gyur pa rnams bshams so// dge bsnyen rnams/ 
8a3(mdo sde): kyis/ sangs rgyas dang / dge 'dun la bsod snyoms rnam pa sna tshogs bshams pa yang / thams cad tsan dan dang / a ga ru'i shing bsrung can bsregs te/ yon tan brgyad dang
8a4(mdo sde): ldan pa'i chu las g.yos su byas so// zhal zas de dag kyi dang ro rnam pa drug dang ldan no// 'di lta ste/ kha ba dang / skur ba dang / dang ra ba dang / tsha ba dang / lan tsha bro ba dang / 
8a5(mdo sde): bsil ba'i ro dang ldan no// gzhan yang yon tan rnam pa gsum dang ldan te/ mnyen zhing 'jam pa dang / gtsang ba/ dang / chos bzhin byas pa'o// de lta bu la sogs pa'i
8a6(mdo sde): mchod pa rnam pa sna tshogs bshams nas/ stobs po che 'byung ba'i gnas sa la'i shing drung du lhag so// gzhan yang gser gyi bye mas sa gzhir bdal te/ lha'i na bza' ka tsa lin da dang / 
8a7(mdo sde): kham pa la dang / dar gyis de'i steng du bting ba ni/ kho ra khor yug dpag tshad bcu gnyis tshun chad yog par byas so// sangs rgyas dang dge 'dun bzhugs pa'i rin po che sna bdun gyi seng ge
8a8(mdo sde): khri bshams te/ khri de dag kyang 'phang du mtho khyad ri rab lhun po dang mnyamo// khri de dag gi stong na rin po che'i gur phub nas/ do shal rnam pa mang po sbyangs// sa la'i shing de dag la yang rnam pa
8b1(mdo sde): sna tshogs kyi ba dar smras te/ gdugs bres nas rnam pa sna tshogs kyi spros bsung can gyi'ang 'gus shing de dag la bskus so// shing gi bar yang me tog rnam pa sna tshogs kyis chal par bka
8b2(mdo sde): dge bsnyen de rnams so so nas yid la 'di snyam du sems so// so so'i skye bo dag gal te bza' bas brel na bza' ba sbyin no// btung bas brel pa la btung ba/ mgo 'dod pa rnams la mgo// mig
8b3(mdo sde): 'dod pa rnams la mig/ de ltar so so'i skye bo dag ci 'dod pa bzhin du thams cad sbyin pa byin te/ sbyin pa de yang / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang / rnyog pa'i sems med do// de la/ 
8b4(mdo sde): gzhan pa 'jig rten gyi longs spyod kyi phyir/ bsam pa'i sems mod kyi/ bla na med pa yong su dag pa'i byang chub 'ba' shi ga gi phyiraro// dge bsnyen de dag bla na med pa'i byang chub la bde
8b5(mdo sde): bar gnas nas/ yang 'di snyam du sems so// de bzhin gshegs pa ni/ bdag cag gi mchod pa 'ang bzhes nas// / yongasu mya ngan las 'da'o snyam bsams nas/ de dag gi
8b6(mdo sde): lus kyi ba spu kun langs te/ lus khrag gis rgyas pa ni/ me tog pa la sha lta bur gyur/ mchi mas ni mig gang / sdug bsngal chen pos ni gdungs par gyur te/ so so nas mchod pa'i yo byad
8b7(mdo sde): bshams pa/ spos kyi shing dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs dang / zhal zas kyi rnam pa rin po che'i shing rtas bskyas nas/ sangs rgyas gang na ba der song ste/ phyin pa dang / 
8b8(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod de/ lan brgya stong du bskor nas skad phyung ste nguso// ngu ba'i sgras gnam sa yang
9a1(mdo sde): g.yos so// brang rdung zhing cho 'debs te mchi ma char bzhin du zag nas/ gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ kyi hud kyi hung grogs po dag 'jig rten stongs// 'jig rten
9a2(mdo sde): stongs so zhes smras nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan sngar lus brdabs te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pas thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ bdag cag
9a3(mdo sde): gis mchod pa bshams pa/ nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das dus mkhyen pa cang mi gsung ste ma bzhes nas/ de bzhin du lan gsum gyi bar du gsol kyang
9a4(mdo sde): bzhi su ma gnang ngo // dge bsnyen de dag bsam pa bzhin du mya gyur nas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te cang mi smra bar 'khong pa ni/ dper na pha ma shin tu byams pa'i bu cig pa/ 
9a5(mdo sde): glo bur du nad kyis btab ste/ tshe 'phos nas/ dur du bskul te/ shin tu mya ngan gyis yid gdungs pa dang 'dra bar/ dge/ bsnyen de dag mya ngan gyis yid gdungs pa yang de dang 'dra ste
9a6(mdo sde): mchod pa'i yo byad rnams gnas gcig tu gzhag nas// phyogs gcig tu cang mi smra bar 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klang gang+gA gsum gyi bye ma snyed kyi dge bsnyen ma khrims lnga yongasu srung ba/ 
9a7(mdo sde): spyod lam dang ldan pa la 'di lta ste/ dge bsnyen ma 'tshe ba'i yon tan dang / dge bsnyen ma dpal gyi 'phreng ba dang / dge bsnyen ma phye ba'i zer sha ka la sogs pas thog mar drangs nas/ dag
9a8(mdo sde): bsnyen ma brgyad khri bzhi stong snyed thams cad kyang / dam pa'i chos yongasu 'dzin pa/ sems can tshad med pa brgya stong gdul ba'i phyir/ bud med kyi lus su ston cing / khyim gyi chos yongs su
9b1(mdo sde): slong ba bdag gi lus la sbrul gdug pa bzhi dang 'dra bar rtogs pa/ lus la rtag tu srin bu grangs med pa zab dang / lus 'di la shin tu bzlog pa dang / 'dod pas yongasu bcings par rtogs/ 
9b2(mdo sde): pa/ lus 'di la khyi ro dang 'dra bar 'jigs su rung ba dang / lus 'di ni mi gtsang ba ste/ bu ga dgu nas rtag tu zag par rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni mkhar dang 'dra ste/ sha dang lpags pa dang / 
9b3(mdo sde): rtswa dang / rgyus pas rnam par dkris pa/ lag pa dang rkang pa ni mkhar gyi nyen lta bur gyur pa/ mig ni skar khung lta bur gyur pa/ mgo bo ni khang pa lta bur gyur te/ sems rgyal po dang 'dra ba/ 
9b4(mdo sde): de'i nang na gnas par rtogs pa/ lus 'khar dang 'dra ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yod su spangs te/ bus pa so so'i skye bo dag ni de la chags par
9b5(mdo sde): byed do// 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi srin po gnas par rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni snying po med pa ste/ 'dam bu'i myu gu'am/ e ran 'da' 'am/ chu'i chu bur ram
9b6(mdo sde): chu shing lta bur rtogs pas/ lus 'di ni mi rtag pa ste/ skad cig skad cig tu 'pho zhing / dper na glog gi 'od dam/ gzar po'i chu 'am/ sgyu ma 'am/ smig rgyu 'am/ chu la ri mor bris pa lta bur
9b7(mdo sde): / rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni 'gyur zhing 'pho ba ste/ dper na chu 'gram g.yang sa'i sdong po lta bur rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni ring por mi thogs pa ste/ spyang ki dang / pher ba dang / srin bya dang / 'ug pa dang / 
9b8(mdo sde): bya rgod dang / khwa dang / ske ga dang / khyi ltogs pa'i zan du gyur te/ 'di la mkhas pa shes can su zhig mos shing chags par byed snyam du rtogs pa/ ba rmig gi nang du rgya mtsho chen po'i chu bluH
10a1(mdo sde): kyang bzod kyi/ lus 'di mi rtag pa dang / mi gtsang ba dang / bzlog pa ni brjod slal ma yin par rtogs pa/ sa chen po'ang rgya shug tsam du dril tam/ chung ngun yungs
10a2(mdo sde): kar gyi 'bru'am/ rdul phra mor gse ba ni sla'i/ lus 'di'i nyes pa'i skyon brjod pa ni sla ba ma yin par rtogs pa/ de bas na mchil ma dang 'dra bar yangs su spangs nas/ de'i rgyu de'i rkyen
10a3(mdo sde): gyis/ dge bsnyen ma rnams stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i chos la rtag tu nan tan byed pa/ theg pa chen po'i mdo sde nyan cing 'dzin pa la mos pa/ thos nas
10a4(mdo sde): kyang gzhan la rgya cher ston nus pa/ sngon gyi smon lam yod/ su 'dzin pa/ bud med kyi lus la shin tu spyad pa/ shin tu skyon che bar shes pa/ snying po med par rtogs pa
10a5(mdo sde): sems ca la 'byor du spyod pa/ de bzhin du yang dag par rtogs cing mtha' med par 'khor ba'i rgyun yongasu gtsu da pa/ theg pa chen po la skom pas gdungs pa ltar mos pa/ 
10a6(mdo sde): bdag shin tu ngoms pas/ gzhan yang shin tu ngoms par byed pa/ theg pa chen po la rab tu mos pa/ theg pa chen po shin tu srung ba/ bud med kyi lus su ston kyang yang dag par byang chub
10a7(mdo sde): sems dpa' sha stag ste/ thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi bsam pa dang / shin tu sbyor ba/ ma rgal ba sgrol ba/ ma grol ba 'grel pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad pa 'chab
10a8(mdo sde): pa/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus chos kyi 'khor lo skor bar 'gyur ba/ rgyan chen pos yongasu brgyan pa/ tshul khrims yongs su srung ba/ de lta bu'i yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can
10b1(mdo sde): thams cad la snying rje'i sems bskyed cing / bu gcig dang 'dra bar gnyi su med par mnyam pa sha stag go// de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma thog ma shar ba na/ 'od kyis reg nas gcig la gcig ni
10b2(mdo sde): skad du/ deng ni shing sa la drung gnyis kyi drung du 'deng ngo // zhes smras so// dge bsnyen ma rnams kyi mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa/ snga ma bas phyed kyis bzang bar sbyar te/ sangs rgyas
10b3(mdo sde): gang na bar lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das
10b4(mdo sde): bdag cag gis/ sangs rgyas dang dge 'dun du bcas kyi la/ mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa 'di/ de bzhin gshegs pas thugs brtse ba'i slad du bzhes shig ces
10b5(mdo sde): gsol to// de la bcom ldan 'das cang mi gsung bar bzhes su ma gnang ngo // dge bsnyen ma rnams bsams ba bzhin ma gyur pas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te/ 
10b6(mdo sde): phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA bzhi'i bye ma snyed kyi li tsa byi'i bu/ grong khyer yangs pa can na gnas pa'i skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang / bu mo dang
10b7(mdo sde): chung ma dang / 'khor rnams dang / gzhan yang 'dzom bu'i gling gi rgyal rig su gtogs pa/ rgyal po'i 'khor dang bcas te thams cad kyang / chos 'dod pa'i phyir/ tshul khrims yod/ 
10b8(mdo sde): su bsrung ba/ spyod lam dang ldan pa/ slob pa gzhan la zhugs shing / dam pa'i chos la sun 'byin pa shin tu tshar gcod pa sha stag gcig la gcig 'di skad ces dam 'cha'o// bdag cag
11a1(mdo sde): gser dang dngul dang / rin po che'i gter mdzod lta bur/ yang dag pa'i chos shin tu bab mo 'dud rtsi lta bu bang mi shes pa/ sum tu 'jig rten na gnas par byas te/ 
11a2(mdo sde): bdag cag kyang de dag la rtag tu nan tan spyod par gyur cig/ gal te zhal nas gsungs pa'i dam pa'i chos la/ dbang za zhing skur pa zhig yod na/ bdag cag gis de'i lce gtsang zhes
11a3(mdo sde): ngam bcas shing / gzhan yang khyim nas/ khyim ma yin par rab tu byung ba dag/ tshul khrims las nyams par gyur na/ bdag cag gis khyim par phab ste/ las byed du gzhug go zhes pa dang / 
11a4(mdo sde): gal te dam pa'i chos la nan tan du byed na/ bdag cag gis bi ma dang 'dra bar/ rim gro dang / bkur sti bya'o zhes pa dang / gal te dge 'dun las dam pa'i chos la nan tan du spyod
11a5(mdo sde): zhig yod na/ bdag cag gis rje su ya~M rang zhing de la mthu yang sbyin par bya'o// zhes dam bcas pa/ rtag tu theg pa chen de'i mdo sde thos par mos shing / thos nas kyang gzhan la
11a6(mdo sde): rgyas par ston pa de lta bu'i yon tan dang ldan pa sha stag la 'di lta ste/ l-i tsa byi'i bu rnam dag dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / li tsa bya'o bu bag yod pa rnam par dag pa dang / li tsa byi'i bu rtag tu dri
11a7(mdo sde): med rnam dag yon tan la sogs te/ de dag gcig gcig 'di skad du/ kye grogs po dag myur bar de bzhin gshegs pa gang na ba der song ste/ mchod pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa sna tshog
11a8(mdo sde): kyis mchod du 'deng ngo // de nas li tsa byi de dag re res kyang / bal glang brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / rin po che'i shing rta/ rta bzhi la bcas pa brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po
11b1(mdo sde): che brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / gzhan yang shing tsan dan dang / a ga ru sbrams pa brgyad khri bzhi stong skyed bshams te/ bal glang de re re'i mdun na rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan
11b2(mdo sde): dang / gdugs kyang bshams so// gdugs nang gi chu ngu yang kho ra khor yug tu dang ga tshad gcig kheng so// ba dan nang gi chung yang ring khyung dang ga tshang sum cu rtsa gnyis so// rin po
11b3(mdo sde): rgyal mtshan nang gi chu nga yang mtho khyang dpag tshad brgya pa ste/ de lta bu'i mchod pa'i yo byad bshams nas/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags te/ phyin pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi
11b4(mdo sde): bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor te/ bcom da ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis sangs rgyas dang / dge slong gi
11b5(mdo sde): dge 'dun rnams la/ mchod pa'i yo byad 'di dag dbul na/ de bzhin gshegs pas bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ mchod pa 'di dag bzhes shig
11b6(mdo sde): ces gsol to// de la de bzhin gshegs pa cang mi gsung nas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // li tsa bya'i bu rnams bsams pa bzhin ma gyur nas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis non te/ bcom
11b7(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis byin gyi rlabs kyis/ sa las shing ta la bdun srid tsam du 'phags nas/ steng gi na mkha' la cang mi smra bar 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA lnga'i bye ma snyed kyi blon
11b8(mdo sde): bo chen po dang / khyim bdag dang / tshong dpon theg pa chen po la shin tu mos pas/ slob pa gzhan la zhugs pa gang zhig yang dag pa'i chos la smod pa zhig yid na/ de dag gi mthus thul ba
12a1(mdo sde): ni/ ji ltar rna ba dang / shing la ser ba bab pa lta bu sha stag la 'di lta ste/ tshong dpon nyi ma'i 'ong dang / tshong dpon 'jig rten skyong dang / tshang dpon chos snong la sogs
12a2(mdo sde): pas thog mar drangs te/ de dag gis so so nas mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa ni/ snga ma bas lnga 'gyur tsam bshams te/ shing sa la drung gnyis kyi bar gang na ba der song ste/ phyin
12a3(mdo sde): pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis/ 
12a4(mdo sde): sangs rgyas dang dge slong gi dge 'dun rnams la/ mchod pa'i yo byad 'di dag 'bul na/ bzhes shig ces gsol to// de la de bzhin gshegs pas cang mi gsung
12a5(mdo sde): nas gzhes su ma gnang ngo // tshong dpon de dag bsams pa bzhin ma gyur nas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis yid gdungs par gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyis
12a6(mdo sde): rlabs kyis/ sa las shing ta la bdun srid du 'phags nas/ steng gi na mkha' la cang mi smra bar 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang yul yangs pa can gyi rgyal po/ btsun mo dang / sra su bcas
12a7(mdo sde): gzhan yang 'dzam bu gling na rgyal po ma skyes dgra ma gtogs par/ rgyal phran de ma yin pa thams cad dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / grong 'dab thams cad kyi mi thams cad dang bcas/ 
12a8(mdo sde): pal 'di lta ste/ rgyal po zla 'od dri med rgyal po la sogs pas thog mar drangs nas/ so so nas dmag rnam bzhi dang bcas te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags so// rgyal po de dag re re
12b1(mdo sde): yang 'khor khri phrag brgyad cu dang bcas so// dmag gi tshogs kyang bal glang dang / d+hU ba ste/ bal glang de dag kyang mche ba drug dang ldan la/ rta rnams kyang mgyogs khyang rlung bzhin te/ 
12b2(mdo sde): mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa yang snga ma bas drug 'gyur gyis lhag go/ rin po che'i gdugs nang gi chu ngu yang / chu zheng kha ra khor yug tu dpag tshad brgyang khebs so// ba dan nang gi thung / 
12b3(mdo sde): du yang ring khyad dpag tshad bcu drug snyeng ngo // rin po che'i rgyal mtshan nang gi chung ngu yang mtha khyang dpag tshod sum cu rtsa drug go// rgyal po de dag thams cad kyang / yang dag pa'i chos la gnas
12b4(mdo sde): pas log pa'i chos kun la shin tu smod pa/ theg pa chen po dal bkur sti byed pa/ theg pa chen po la shin tu dmos pa/ sems can thams cad bu cig dang 'dra bar byams
12b5(mdo sde): pa/ zhal zas bshams pa'i dri yang dpag tshad bzhi'i bar du khro ba bshams nas/ snga dro'i dus kyi tshe mchod pa'i yo byad rnam pa sna tshogs thogs te/ shing sa la drung gnyis
12b6(mdo sde): kyi bar de bzhin gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa der song nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis/ sangs rgyas dang / dge slong
12b7(mdo sde): gi dge 'dun rnams la mchod pa 'di dag 'bul na/ de bzhin gshegs pas thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ bdag cag gi mchod pa tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs
12b8(mdo sde): pa dus mkhyen pas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // rgyal po de dag kyang bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur pas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis yid gdungs par gyur te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i
13a1(mdo sde): gzhan yang klung gang+gA bdun gyi bye ma snyed kyi rgyal po'i btsun mo rnams tshogs te/ de la gcig ma gtogs pa ni/ ma skyes dgra'i btsun ma 'ba' shig go/ sam
13a2(mdo sde): can gdul ba'i phyir/ bud med kyi lus su ston te/ rtag tu lus kyis nan tan tu spyod cing / stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i chos la sems 'dris shing gams
13a3(mdo sde): par byed pa de la sogs te/ btsun mo khams gsum bzang mo dang / btsun mo 'dod pa'i yon tan la sogs pas thogs drangs so// thams cad kyang dam pa'i chos la gnas shing / tshul
13a4(mdo sde): khrims yongs su srung ba/ spyod lam dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la bu gcig pa dang 'dra bar byams pa sha stag go/ de dag kyang gcig la gcig 'di skad du
13a5(mdo sde): bdag cag kyang myur bar sangs rgyas gang na bzhugs par 'dong ngo zhes smras so// rgyal po'i btsun mo rnams kyi/ sa mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa ni/ snga ma bas bdun
13a6(mdo sde): 'gyur gyis lhag ste/ me tog dang / spos dang / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / dar gyi ba dan dang / gdugs dang / zhal zas mchog rnams so// rin po che'i gdugs nang gi
13a7(mdo sde): chu ngu yang / chu zheng kho ra khor yug tu dpag tshad bcu drug khebs so// ba dan nang gi chu nga tshad kyang dpag tshad sum cu rtsa drug snyed do// rin po che'i rgyal mtshan nang gi dma' ba'i tshad kyang
13a8(mdo sde): dpag tshad drug cu rtsa brgyad snyed do// zhal zas kyi dri bsung gis kyang dpag tshad brgyad kyi bar du bro ba/ mchod pa'i yo byad de lta bu dag bshams nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba
13b1(mdo sde): der song ste phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du ma bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das/ 
13b2(mdo sde): bdag cag gis sangs rgyas dang / dge slong gi dge 'dun rnams la/ mchod pa'i yo byad bshams te/ 'bul ba 'di/ de bzhin gshegs pas bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i
13b3(mdo sde): slang du mchod pa nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes cig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs po dus mkhyen pas/ cang mi gsung nas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // de'i tshe rgyal po'i btsun
13b4(mdo sde): mo rnams bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur nas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te skra 'bal zhing / drang dal thal mos rdebs te/ cho nges rdung ba ni/ ji ltar bu'i
13b5(mdo sde): nang na sdug pa shi ba dang 'dra bar gyur nas/ phyogs gcig tu cang mi smra bar 'khod ngo // de'i tshe klung gang+gA brgyad kyi bye ma snyed kyi lha'i bu mo rnams la 'di lta ste/ 
13b6(mdo sde): lha'i bu mo yangs pa'i mig ces bya bas/ thog mar drangs te 'di skad ces smras// kye grogs mo dag mthong ngem ltos shig/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mang pos mchod pa'i yo byad
13b7(mdo sde): rnam pa sna tshogs bshams nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / dge slong gi dge 'dun la 'bul ba mthong ngam/ bdag cag kyang mchod pa'i yo byad bshams te/ de bzhin
13b8(mdo sde): gshegs pa la mchod nas/ de bzhin gshegs pas bzhes pa'i 'og tu/ mya ngan las mi 'da' bar bzhugasu gsol bar bya'o// kye grogs po dag sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
14a1(mdo sde): 'jig rten du gshegs pa yang shin tu dka'/ mchod pas gi tha ma bshams te 'bul ba yang shin tu dka'o// lag te bcom ldan 'das mya ngan las 'das na/ 
14a2(mdo sde): 'jig rten stongs par 'gyur ro// zhes smras so// lha'i bu mo de rnams kyang theg pa chen po 'dod pa/ theg pa chen po thos par mos pa/ thos nas kyang gzhan la rgya cher ston nus pa/ 
14a3(mdo sde): theg pa chen po la skom pas gdungs pa ltar gyur cing bdag shin tu ngoms par byed pa/ skom pas gdungs pa gzhan dag kyang ngoms par byed pa/ theg pa chen po la skyob pa/ slob pa
14a4(mdo sde): gzhan la zhugs pa dag/ thag pa chen po la sun 'byin cing phrag dog byed pa yod na/ ji ltar rtsa la ser ba bab pa bzhin du/ shin tu thul pa/ tshul khrims yongs su
14a5(mdo sde): srung ba/ spyod lam dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten thams da kyi yid dang sbyor ba la shin tu mkhas pa/ ma dul ba rnams 'dul ba/ ma grel pa rnams grol bar byed pa/ 
14a6(mdo sde): phyi ma ma 'ongaso pa'i dus su ches kyi 'khor lo skor zhing / dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad par 'tshe ba pa/ theg pa chen po la nan tan byed cing / rgyan chen pos shin tu
14a7(mdo sde): brgyan pa/ de lta bu'i yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la yang bu cig dang 'dra bar byams pa sha stag ste/ de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma thog ma shar pa na/ 
14a8(mdo sde): so so nas rnam pa sna tshogs kyi lha'i shing bsung can bshams pa ni/ mi'i shing bsung can las khyad par du gyur pa shing gi bsung nges/ mi'i 'jig rten na mnam zhing dri mi zhim pa
14b1(mdo sde): thams cad zhi bar byed pa/ shing rta dkar po la gdugs pa/  po bres te/ rta dkar po bzhis drangs pa/ shing rta re re ro'i steng yang gur dkar po phub pa la gur gyi mtha' ma yang gser gyi
14b2(mdo sde): dril bu sbyangs pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyi spos dang / me tog dang / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs dang / zhal zas mchog dam pa dang rol mo rnam pa sna tshogs
14b3(mdo sde): bshams te/ seng ge'i gdan bting ngo // seng ge'i gdan gyi rkang pa bzhi yang / bai dUr+ya mthon ting las byas pa/ de'i rgyab ni rin po che sna bdun gyi snam rten dang bcas pa la/ mdun/ 
14b4(mdo sde): yang gser la byas pa'i sngas re re yod pa/ rin po che sna bdu na gyi sgron ma'i sdong po la/ nor bu rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sprin ma spang ba/ sa gzhi thams cad lha'i me hA
14b5(mdo sde): gis chal par bkod pa de lta bu dag/ lha'i bu mo de dag gi/ sa bshams nas/ yid gdungs zhing mchi ma zag/ ste/ sdug bsngal chen po skyes kyang / sems can thams
14b6(mdo sde): cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ theg pa chen po don dam pa stong pa nyid dang ldan par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pas dgongs te gsungs pa mngon du bstan pa dang / chos rnam pa sna
14b7(mdo sde): tshogs smra ba rgyun mi bcad pa'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gang na bar lhags nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong du ma bskor nas/ bcom ldan
14b8(mdo sde): 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du mchod pa bshams po'i nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das dus ma
15a1(mdo sde): / pas cang mi gsung nas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // lha'i bu mo rnams bsams pa bzhin ma gyur nas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te cang mi smra bar phyogs gcig tu 'khod
15a2(mdo sde): do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klang gang ga dgu'i bye ma snyed kyi klu'i rgyal po phyogs bzhi nas lhags pa la 'di lta ste/ klu'i rgyal po 'jog po dang / klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang / klu'i rgyal po bsnyen
15a3(mdo sde): dga' bo la sogs pas theg mar drangs nas/ klu'i rgyal po rnams kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma thog mar shar pa na/ lha dang mi las lhag pa'i mchod pa'i yo byad bshams nas/ bcom ldan
15a4(mdo sde): 'das gang na bar lhags te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhab das la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du ma bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces
15a5(mdo sde): gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du mchod pa'i nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes/ shig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dus mkhyen
15a6(mdo sde): pas cang mi gsung nas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // de nas klu'i rgyal po rnams kyang bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur pas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe
15a7(mdo sde): gzhan yang klung gang ga bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po ngal bso po la sogs pas thog mar drangs nas/ gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ kye skyes bu dag myur bar sangs rgyas
15a8(mdo sde): gang na bder 'ding ngo // zhes smras nas/ mchod po'i yo byad klu bas lhag par bshams te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na bar lhags nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag
15b1(mdo sde): 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong du ma bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ mchod pa bshams
15b2(mdo sde): pa'i nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// de la bcom ldan 'das cang mi gsung bas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po rnams bsams pa bzhin ma gyur pas/ 
15b3(mdo sde): mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod // de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA nyi shu'i bye ma snyed kyi na mkha' lding gi rgyal po phas rgol ba bcom pa zhes bya bas thog mar
15b4(mdo sde): drangs so// gzhan yang glung gang gsum cu'i bye ma snyed kyi dri za'i rgyal po mthu bo ches thog mar drangs de so// gzhan yang klung gang+ga bzhi bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi mi
15b5(mdo sde): 'am ci'i rgyal po shin tu mthong ba zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang+gA lnga bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi lto 'phye chen po'i rgyal po shin tu mthong ba chen po
15b6(mdo sde): zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung drug cu'i bye ma snyed kyi lha ma yin gyi rgyal po kham ba lis thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang+gA bdun cu'i bye ma snyed kyi ta na pa'i
15b7(mdo sde): rgyal po dri med 'bab chu dang / ba ti da ta la sogs pas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang+gA brgyad cu'i bye ma snyed kyi srin po'i rgyal po 'jig su rung ba zhes bya bas thog mar drangs/ 
15b8(mdo sde): de dag kyang sdig pa mi dge ba'i sems yongs su spangs nas/ mi la mi za ba dang / dgra dang khon tu gyur pa la byams shing snying rje'i sems skye ba dang / gzugs mi sdug pa yang sangs rgyas
16a1(mdo sde): kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis thams cad bzang zhing sdug par gyur to// gzhan yang klung gang+gA dgu bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi nags tshal la dbang ba'i lha dri gsung la dga' ba/ 
16a2(mdo sde): zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang+ga stong gi bye ma snyed kyi rig 'dzin gyi rgyal po rdzu 'phrul chen po zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang+gA 'bum gyi bye ma
16a3(mdo sde): snyed kyi mdangs za ba'i rgyal po shin tu mthong zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang ga khri phrag brgya'i bye ma snyed kyi lha'i bu mo 'dod chags can lam pa dang / ur pa shi
16a4(mdo sde): dang / te lo tsa ma dang / phyir sha ka la sogs pa sa thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang ga khri phrag stong gi bye ma snyed kyi sa la gnas pa'i yi dgas kyi
16a5(mdo sde): rgyal po gzhog dkar zhes bya bas thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang ga 'bum phrag bcu'i bye ma snye/ dkyi lha'i sras po rnams dang / lha'i rgyal po la phyogs
16a6(mdo sde): bzhi'i mgon pos thog mar drangs so// gzhan yang klung gang ga 'bum phrag bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi rlung gi lhas ni phyogs bzhi nas sa las skyes pa'i me tog dus dang / dus ma yin pa
16a7(mdo sde): rnams sa la'i shing drung du chal par bkang ngo // gzhan yang klung gang ga 'bum phrag bcu'i bye ma snyed kyi rlung dang / char la dbang ba'i lha rnams ni 'di snyam du/ bdag cag gis

16b1(mdo sde): kyang shin tu bsil bar bya'o// snyam du sems so// gnan yang klung gang gnyi shu'i bye ma snyed kyi spos kyi bal glang chen po bal glang gi rgyal po la bu dang / bal glang gi rgyal po gser
16b2(mdo sde): can dang / bal glang gi rgyal po dang ra ba'i ro dang / bal glang gi rgyal po mthon ting mig dang / bal glang gi rgyal po bsung can la sogs pas thog mar drangs te/ de dag thams ca
16b3(mdo sde): kyang theg po chen po la sti stang byed pa/ theg pa chen po la mos pa sha stag ste/ de dag gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ring por mi thogs par mya ngan las 'das par shes
16b4(mdo sde): pas/ so so nas pad+mo bzang po tshad med pa dpag tu me dad pa phyung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang na bar lhags nas/ gdong gi phyag 'tshal te phyogs gcig
16b5(mdo sde): tu sdong ngo // gzhan yang klung gang gnyi shu'i bye ma snyed/ kyi ri dgas kyi rgyal po seng ge seng ge sgra zhes bya bas thog mar drangs te/ sems can thams cad la mi 'jigs
16b6(mdo sde): pa byin nas/ so so nas me tog dang 'bras bu thogs te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu sdong ngo // gzhan yang
16b7(mdo sde): rlung gang gnyi shu'i bye ma snyed kyi bya'i rgyal po ngang pa dang / ngur pa dang / rma bya dang / 'gen dar ba dang / ka lan ta dang / gu yog dang / ne tse dang / kau shi la dang / ba hi ka dang / 
16b8(mdo sde): ka la bing ka dang / 'tsho byed 'tsho byed la sogs pa/ bya'i rgyal po rnams kyang / so so nas me tog dang / 'bras bu thogs te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ 
17a1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la phag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu sdod do// gzhan yang klung gang gnyi shu'i bye ma snyed kyi chu glang dang / ba dang lug la sogs
17a2(mdo sde): patasangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ grong khyer rtse mchog gi 'obs dang / shang shong thams cad kyang dri bsung dang ldan pa/ kha dog dang / ro bro bar ldan pa'i 'o mas kun tu gang
17a3(mdo sde): bar byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu sdod do// gzhan yang klung gang ga nyi shu'i bye ma snyed kyi gling bzhi la gnas pa'i drang srong bzod pa can zhes bya ba la sogs pas thog mar drangs te/ so so
17a4(mdo sde): nas me tog dang / spos dang 'bras bu dang ra ba la sogs dpa thogs te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/

17a6(mdo sde): shig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dus mkhyen pas cang mi gsung nas bzhes su ma gnang nas/ drang srong rnams bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur nas/ mya ngan gyis yid
17a7(mdo sde): gdungs te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// 'dzam bu gling gi bung ba'i rgyal po sgra snyan ces bya bas thog mar drangs nas/ bung ba thams cad kyang me tog rnam pa sna tshogs thogs te/ sangs
17a8(mdo sde): rgyas gang na bor lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ lan gcog bskor nas phyogs gcig tu sdong ngo // de'i tshe 'dzam bu'i gling ni gnas pa'i dge slong dang
17b1(mdo sde): dge slong ma thams cad 'dus te/ de la gnyis ma gtogs pa ni/ 'od srung chen po dang dga' bo'o// gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med grangs med pa klung gang+gA'i bye ma
17b2(mdo sde): snyed dang / 'dzam bu'i gling gau ri la sogs pa/ ri rab ri'i rgyal pos thog mar drangs te/ ri de dag thams cad kyang shin tu brgyan pa ni nags tshal rgyas pa dang / shing rnams kyi lo ma
17b3(mdo sde): dang yal ga yang ran par nyi ma'i 'od chod pa dang / me tog rnam pa sna tshogs rgyas pa dang / kho ra khor yug tu 'bang chu dang / chu mig yongs su dag cing / gsung dang ldan pa dang
17b4(mdo sde): lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin/ dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto da'aphye chen po dang / rig 'dzin dang / drang srong la sogs
17b5(mdo sde): pas/ rol mo rnam pa sna tshogs byed pas yongs su gang bar gyur to// lha dang drang srong de dag kyang / bcom ldan 'das gang na bar lhags te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs
17b6(mdo sde): la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// gzhan yang grangs med pa'i klung gang+gA'i bye ma snyed kyi rgya mtsho bzhi'i lha dang / 'bab chu kun gyi lha gzi brjid chen po dang ldan pa/

17b8(mdo sde): sdong bar byas nas/ me tog tsam pa kas klung ha ril pa ti logs su gtor te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu
